    <script>
//<![CDATA[

(function () {
    var w=window,d=document,l,r,kc,t,
    sbox = d.getElementsByName("p")[0],
    sBdr = d.getElementById('fp-search-bdr'),
    sBdrClasses = sBdr.className,
    sBdrFocusClass = " brdr-focus",
    checkFocus = function (e) {
        try {
            kc = e.keyCode;
            t = (e.target) ? e.target : e.srcElement;
            l = sbox.value.length;
            if (t === sbox && l === 0 && (kc >= 32 && kc <= 40)) {
                sbox.blur();
            } else if (t.tagName !== 'EMBED' && t.tagName !== 'OBJECT' && t.tagName !== 'INPUT' && t.tagName !== 'TEXTAREA' && !e.altKey && !e.metaKey && !e.ctrlKey && (kc < 32 || kc > 40) && kc != 9 && kc != 13 && kc != 16) {
                if (l) {
                    if (sbox.setSelectionRange) {
                        sbox.setSelectionRange(l,l);
                    } else if (sbox.createTextRange) {
                        r = sbox.createTextRange();
                        r.moveStart('character', l);
                        r.select();
                    }
                }
                sbox.focus();
            }
        } catch(e) {}
    },
    focusInput = function (e) {
        sBdr.className += sBdrFocusClass;
    };
    blurInput = function (e) {
        sBdr.className = sBdrClasses;
    };

    if (sbox) {
        if (w.addEventListener) {
            w.addEventListener('keydown', checkFocus, false);
            sbox.addEventListener('focus', focusInput, true);
            sbox.addEventListener('blur', blurInput, true);
        } else if (w.attachEvent)  {
            d.attachEvent('onkeydown', checkFocus);
            sbox.attachEvent('onfocus', focusInput);
            sbox.attachEvent('onblur', blurInput);
        }
        setTimeout(function(){
                sbox.focus();//so this works onload.
                
perfLog = (function(){
    var perfImages = {};
        return function(){
            var img = new Image(),
                querystring = "",
                time;

            /*
             * Image management. Sometimes IE will cancel requests prematurely due
             * to the destruction of the image object.
             */
            perfImages['img'] = img;
            img.onload = img.onerror = function(){
                delete perfImages['img'];
            };
            time = Number(new Date());
            querystring= 'inputFocus=' + (time - rtTop);
            img.src = '/perf.gif' + "?" + querystring;

            return querystring;
        }();
}());
            }, 1000);
    }
})();

//]]>
    </script>

                              <a class="" href="http://hsrd.yahoo.com/_ylt=A2KLtd.I74NTR8EAnrObvZx4;_ylu=X3oDMTN1cmZudWU3BGJwb3MDMQRjY29kZQNkd2hfbG9nZ2VyBGNwb3MDMQRjdAMxBGcDNjE5MTQzY2YtNjFmMi0zOWM1LWFkMjUtYTRkYzg4M2M2NjYzBGludGwDdXMEcGtndAM0BHBvcwMxBHNlYwN0ZC1zdHJtBHNsawN0aXRsZQR0ZXN0AzkwMQ--/RV=1/RE=1402365064/RH=aHNyZC55YWhvby5jb20-/RO=2/RU=aHR0cDovL25ld3MueWFob28uY29tL21leGljYW4tbWFuLW9uY2Utd29ybGRzLWhlYXZpZXN0LWRpZXMtNDgtMTg0NjQ1MTYwLmh0bWw-/RS=^ADAHxPKwduCCqyv.xIya3WuUBjhFLI-" data-ylk="sec:strm;cat:default;bpos:1;cpos:1;pkgt:4;slk:title;sort:1;ct:1;rspns:nav;">

                              </a>
                            </h3>
                            <p class="summary mt-xxs">
                              MONTERREY, Mexico (AP) ? A Mexican man once listed as the world's heaviest human being died Monday at the age of 48.

                            </h3>
                            <p class="summary mt-xxs">
                              We all like to think of yogurt as a healthy breakfast, but as it turns out, many of the most popular yogurt brands have more sugar than a junk food you'd never consider eating. The American Heart Association recommends that men eat no more than 36 grams of sugar per day, and women no more than 20.
                            </p>
                          </div>
                          <div class="attribution fz-xxs">
                            <span class="source">

                                  Cooking

                            <h3 class="fw-b fz-s lh-115">
                              <a class="" href="http://hsrd.yahoo.com/_ylt=A2KLtd.I74NTR8EAuLObvZx4;_ylu=X3oDMTN2NWx2cW8xBGJwb3MDMQRjY29kZQNkd2hfbG9nZ2VyBGNwb3MDMTgEY3QDMQRnAzRiMGFkNjI5LWNiNTEtM2UwMi05NDcxLTMyYjg0YWY4ZWMyNwRpbnRsA3VzBHBrZ3QDNARwb3MDMQRzZWMDdGQtc3RybQRzbGsDdGl0bGUEdGVzdAM5MDE-/RV=1/RE=1402365064/RH=aHNyZC55YWhvby5jb20-/RO=2/RU=aHR0cDovL3NoaW5lLnlhaG9vLmNvbS9wZXRzL2Nvb3Blci1uaWNvLXR3by1yZXNjdWUtZG9ncy1jaGFuZ2VkLW9uZS13b21hbnMtMTIzODAwNjE0Lmh0bWw-/RS=^ADA5yuXfK6NmdOo33_Lo01QWOWn7.U-" data-ylk="sec:strm;cat:default;bpos:1;cpos:18;pkgt:4;slk:title;sort:1;ct:1;rspns:nav;">
                                Cooper and Nico: How Two Rescue Dogs Changed One Woman's Life
                              </a>
                            </h3>
                            <p class="summary mt-xxs">
                              Katie O'Regan didn't intend to rescue two dogs. In May 2013, O'Regan adopted Cooper and Nico from Warm Fuzzys Cat Rescue, a facility in Tupelo, Miss., that saved the pups from euthanasia. The adorable brothers recently turned 1, and O'Regan says her two pups have changed her life for the better. We
